The nose behind this fragrance is Jacques Polge. Top notes are Quince and Grapefruit; middle notes are Hyacinth and Jasmine; base notes are Musk, Iris, Virginia Cedar and Amber. </p><div v-pre class='fragrantica-blockquote'><p>Chanel is presenting a new flanker of their popular fragrance Chance which arrives on the market on April 2nd 2010. The romantic and pink new version, Chance Eau Tendre, is announced as a floral-fruity interpretation of Chance EDP.
</p>

The huge downside is that she is a runner.  Longevity is absolutely terrible, resulting in me being almost out of the bottle just a few months after buying it due to necessary over spraying to keep her alive.  It is truly "tender," both in it's scent profile, but also in its fleeting nature. I'm currently contemplating a repurchase, and am very much on the fence, as they've also been slowly but surely increasing the price.  The other huge downside is that this fragrance is ubiquitous, and I constantly smell it on others.  It's great that so many people like it, but who wants to smell like another girl?  I would consider this an inoffensive, wear anywhere perfume, but was told by a coworker recently that I smelled like his Ex.  Ouch (for both of us).  That comment alone is making me lean towards a "no" on the re-up.  Maybe I'll just enjoy smelling it on others.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="8069"comment_id="2312116"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Chance-Eau-Tendre-8069.html?ccid=2312116#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2306921" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It's not exactly the same, but it's close enough for my purposes. I had a sample from Chanel, and it was difficult to tell the difference between this and the Maison Alhambra dupe fifteen minutes into the drydown. They both start with piquant grapefruit notes and soften into a clean-girl musky floral. The effect is more of a generalized bouquet than distinctive notes of individual flowers--a pity because I adore hyacinth. When I have Chanel money to spend, I'll save it for one of their more distinctive offerings, like Polge's gorgeous Coco (the OG, not Mademoiselle). Chance Eau Tendre is undeniably pretty, though.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="8069"comment_id="2290696"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Chance-Eau-Tendre-8069.html?ccid=2290696#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2290598" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2290598" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="LadyLane83"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2206488"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2206488.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="LadyLane83" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Issey-Miyake/A-Drop-d-Issey-Eau-de-Parfum-Fraiche-73900.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.73900.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="A Drop d'Issey Eau de Parfum Fraiche"title="A Drop d'Issey Eau de Parfum Fraiche"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2290598ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2290598" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.75); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2206488">LadyLane83</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-21">09/21/24 12:40</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I have gone through multiple dossier dupes of this before I ever had the real thing so that may be coloring my review since acquiring a genuine bottle of this glorious masterpiece…<br />
<br />
I typically go for fresh, clean, florals. Pastel fragrances. Big on rosewater type scents and don’t like my florals to be super sweet fruity. This right here is perfection. It’s so CLEAN. I never understood when someone would describe something as soapy and I never considered it a bad thing. This is soapy. Clean warm soapy bubbles floating all around you with a beautiful iridescent glow. At first spray it is a vibrant grapefruit (a note I am finding I truly love in perfumes) and settles down to a very inviting soft floral. I am obsessed.<br />
<br />
I struggle with silage and longevity, my skin eats perfume and the types of scents I like typically don’t have good longevity anyway but this stuff hits. My bottle is second hand and about three years old, so I don’t know if it just matured to this strength or what but it is STRONG. I am an over sprayer (like 15+ sprays always with everything) and can only spray about 5 sprays of this before it’s too much and it lasts easy 6-8 hours, where as everything else lasts about 2 hours on me. <br />
<br />
1,000% will be buying a bottle directly from Chanel to save and let mature while I annihilate the one I have. <br />
<br />
Also just noticed a base note in this is Virginia Cedar and that happens to also be a base note in my all time favorite discontinued Dior Addict to Life. Might be on to something…</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="8069"comment_id="2290598"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Chance-Eau-Tendre-8069.html?ccid=2290598#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2288743" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Pierwsze na ktore trafiłam to były Chanel 5 i od razu skojarzyły mi się z takim mydlanym zapachem i starsza panią. Chanel Mademoiselle tez jakos mnie nie przekonaly i nie rozumiałam szału na ich punkcie ale....Chance Eau Tendre  poprostu pokochalam. Wyróżniają się świeżym, lekkim i delikatnym charakterem. Grejpfrut oraz pigwa na otwarciu nadają zapachowi soczystości i rześkości, co w połączeniu z kwiatowym sercem (z dominującym jaśminem) sprawia, że całość jest bardzo kobieca i romantyczna. Piżmo i cedr w bazie dodają zapachowi głębi i elegancji, utrzymując jednocześnie subtelny, pudrowy char. Ten zapach jest dla mnie lekki, radosny i pełen pozytywnej energii. Jest idealny dla kobiet, które preferują delikatne, nieinwazyjne, a jednocześnie kobiece perfumy. Idealny na codzień, do pracy, na spotkania w ciągu dnia, ale również na romantyczne wieczory.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="8069"comment_id="2281106"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Chance-Eau-Tendre-8069.html?ccid=2281106#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2280066" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1625667">ripgirl9000</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-24">04/24/24 09:49</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is a youthful scent, and not in a juvenile way, but in a happy bubbly way. It is sweet, fresh and feminine. I fell in love with this scent at 15 and still love it today at 33. I do not think this smell would be offensive to anyone. And while I have many floral / citrus based perfumes, nothing I have smells quite like Chanel Chance Tendre. The main vibe of this perfume is sweet freshness, not too citrus-y and not too floral. A sweet lemony lotion with some floral undertones. A great spring fragrance.<br />
<br />
I have Chanel Chance Eau Fraiche and Eau Tendre. I love them both. The big difference is Fraiche has wood notes and lacks sweetness which makes it a more grounded mature fragrance. Tendre leans happy, bubbly, bright &amp; youthful. While Fraiche leans classy, crisp, luxurious &amp; mature. But they are clearly related when you smell them, so they have the same base profile.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="8069"comment_id="2134960"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Chance-Eau-Tendre-8069.html?ccid=2134960#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2124843" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Elegant enough to be worn in the office or at meetings, yet natural enough with haunting floral notes. Moderate quince notes. The grapefruit is not too strong, it just adds a little "freshness" to the top notes, like freshly fallen rain. <br />
In my memory, it was much "younger" - for this reason, I preferred the eau de parfum. But now, when I consciously perceive the eau de toilette again, I realise that it doesn't smell young at all, but simply pure, lively and innocent. <br />
It is the perfect fragrance if you are looking for a perfume that is not "too much of anything". It's simply there to emphasise your individual style with class while staying true to your natural, enchanting femininity.<br />
For this spring: love.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="8069"comment_id="2063886"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Chance-Eau-Tendre-8069.html?ccid=2063886#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2062528" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1387189">violeteme</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-02-14">02/14/24 10:15</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I currently have EdT and EdP versions sprayed on different wrists. As per usual, Chanel different versions of the same perfume have such minuscule differences, they are barely felt. Truthfully, they probably can be felt only comparing side by side and very attentively analyzing, seeking for these differences. Just by someone passing by, I doubt they are detectible that much at all. Unless, the nose is very well trained.<br />
EdT is just tiny bit fruitier, tiny bit softer, EdP has some rose sharpness, which makes it gently more mature smelling (it is absolutely still Eau Tendre, nowhere near those very mature, robust perfumes anyway). But as I already mentioned, dissimilarities are so extremely tiny. I find their performance the same. <br />
I've read other reviews, I have to agree, I love how uncomplicated, simple, non-pretentious it is. How it smells just simply, effortlessly beautiful. I love the whole aesthetic of the bottle, the color, the box, the presentation. So gracefully feminine and elegant. Unfortunately, also fleeting, it stays on only for 2-3 hours.<br />
<br />
I only now realized that the newer/most flanker creations belong to the nose Olivier Polge, the son of Jacques Polge, who was creating perfumes for Chanel for a long time. EdT is one of his creations and EdP - one of his son's. I have to admire his respect for his father's creations.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="8069"comment_id="2062067"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Chance-Eau-Tendre-8069.html?ccid=2062067#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2060634" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; The opening hits you with an impressive crispy, watery, fruit, note of exotic quince. It's reminiscent of various types of apples but more unique and rare. The dry down transcends into a cosmetic, possibly shampoo scent as others imply. Then the last notes make me think of the original Very Sexy by Victoria's Secret. padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/239364">verzosa</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-11-27">11/27/23 16:14</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>To me EDT vs EDP are very different, but I love both of them. This version is much more energetic, fresh and talks more. The EDP is floral forward with longer longevity whilst still happy with a denser musk. It's also more rose centered, elegant and mature.<br />
<br />
I think the parfum makes more of a statement and knows where it's going. This version is more youthful and sparkly. I love the projection of the white musk in this version as it is perfectly sheer yet bright; I find this characteristic the most prominent. The purple florals are well blended, but does not dominate the scent.<br />
<br />
I get a ridiculous amount of compliments when I wear this, but be weary some people mistake it for my shampoo. For something so fresh it gives off a nice cozy feel.<br />
<br />
While both are very happy and uplifting the EDT sure smells more clean and I find it much more addictive.<br />
<br />
Edit: After some time with the parfum, I do prefer this version. I ended up exchanging the EDP for the EDT. My impulsive side wants both, but my minimal side is telling me it's unnecessary.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="8069"comment_id="1986776"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Chance-Eau-Tendre-8069.html?ccid=1986776#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1975378" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Younger and less sophisticated smelling than Mademoiselle. For tweens up to early 20's (11-23). Where Mademoiselle is the more mature scent for office/formal situations Chance Eau Tendre works better in a casual setting. <br />
<br />
This is a more sophisticated and higher class competitor to Lancôme's Idôle. Where Idôle blasts everyone within a 2 meter radius of Lancôme's loud, cloying synthetic rose scent, this would tantalize you with a higher quality and more natural smelling rose. It's not loud but it would waft in the air with every movement if sprayed in the hair, behind the ear or the neck. <br />
<br />
Speaking of the florals, it's certainly of a higher quality and contains more depth and complexity than Idôle so this is for the classier young lady.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; I sprayed this on my skin two times already, and I’m still liking her. I really want to compare the edt Vs the edp of this perfume. I accidentally didn’t side sprayed it on my arm, but still can faintly smell it. I tried the other Chanel’s, and to me they either smell too old lady (all of the Chanel no 5 line), or they smell almost generic. This one is kind of generic and crowd pleasing to me especially the dry down. However, I might get a bottle of this to see if I’m fully in love with it in the end.<br />
<br />
Summary:<br />
Smells like: A good smelling shampoo, sweet but citrusy. a crowd pleaser.<br />
Family of: Daisy by Marc Jacobs (better version)<br />
Silage: moderate to intimate <br />
<br />
Verdict:<br />
Pass- I looked it up, and this is the best selling perfume in Sephora. I’m not gonna buy a full bottle of this because I’m a hipster that wants to smell more unique. However, I can appreciate it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="8069"comment_id="1885463"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Chance-Eau-Tendre-8069.html?ccid=1885463#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1885430" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1613746">Billford420</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-07-13">07/13/23 07:29</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Tried it on a test strip at Sephora, was not pleased. I then did a skin tests, and it’s lovely.<br />
When I first got this bottle it was just Jasmin sambac that came through, took a few days for everything to settle.<br />
I have no idea what quince smells like, but we open with a slightly green, maybe tea-ish citrus opening.<br />
The hyancinth and jasmine make a for a somewhat darker feel, while at the same time being light and very wearable.<br />
The base is really nice, although its got some longevity issues.<br />
Seeing as how this is never at discounters, I’d say it’s not worth the money. Though if you can find a 100 ml for under 125, I’d say that’s a good deal.<br />
Try before you buy, and make sure you try on your skin first. Buying fragrances based upon test strips is like buying books based upon its cover.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="8069"comment_id="1877701"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Chance-Eau-Tendre-8069.html?ccid=1877701#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1877438" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It's soft but not creamy or powdery, just a soft scent that uplifts.  It leaves a soft trail so others will be aware of it but not burdened with it. Easy to like and suits many. Perhaps boring in the long run. Yet sexy and not intrusive. A great dupe is Zara Apple juice. For a fraction of the money. The real Chanel is a bit more spicy ambery in the drydown. But only a pro will notice. Not very similar to the Marc Jacobs Daisy at all. Daisy has a fattier musky undertone. Chanel is more settled and breathes quality for sure.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="8069"comment_id="1852743"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Chance-Eau-Tendre-8069.html?ccid=1852743#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1852641" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:1,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1845608" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Swagnoodle"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1761317"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="Swagnoodle" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1845608ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1845608" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1761317">Swagnoodle</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-05-31">05/31/23 01:49</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>If I could only pick one single fragrance, regardless of situation and performance, it would easily be Chance Eau Tendre. To me, it has a distinctive light academia aesthetics-vibe over it. Sort of "old money", without being obnoxious or stuck up. Just so damn clean and elegant. It's girly, but the musk provides something more wholesome and mature, like a girl who's wise beyond her years. It also holds the place for the single most romantic fragrance I can think of. Not in a sexy and mysterious kind of way perhaps, it's more like being in love with someone who makes you feel safe. <br />
<br />
My history with Chance Eau Tendre goes way back. I first got it gifted from the grandparents of my first boyfriend back when it was first launched, and I made it my entire personality for a month after getting it; I even sprayed it on my pillow before going to sleep. It wasn't really suitable for my teenage budget though (especially in the manner I used it), so I didn't repurchase until a couple of years had passed. At that time, I was 18 and traveling to Paris with my second boyfriend. It was autumn, and we spent the weekend walking hand in hand between cute little coffee shops. I remember how my scarf smelled like Chance Eau Tendre and how I kept digging my nose into the soft fabric to get a whiff of the fragrance combined with crisp autumnal air. The bf was actually utter trash though, so I consider it to be more of a love affair between me and Paris, but nevertheless - this is what comes to mind when I smell Chance Eau Tendre. <br />
<br />
Luckily, the only thing to change was my taste in men. My love for Chance Eau Tendre still stands ever so strong, despite her slightly weak performance. Because sillage and longevity really isn't all that great - which it honestly should be, given the price point. Still, I keep coming back, keep forgiving. Because there's nothing that makes me feel quite the same. It's floral and light and fresh, but still with that grounding musk note that keeps you down to earth and humble. It's what I'll indefinitely wear when I want to feel like ~that girl~. 4.5/5</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="8069"comment_id="1845608"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Chance-Eau-Tendre-8069.html?ccid=1845608#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1843134" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1809270" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="MomGodess"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1250867"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1250867.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="MomGodess" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Chanel/Chance-Eau-Tendre-8069.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.8069.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Chance Eau Tendre"title="Chance Eau Tendre"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1809270ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck6x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1809270" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.85); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1250867">MomGodess</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-04-15">04/15/23 00:49</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>My husband picked this for me. Such a sweet and weird experience. A couple years ago I had a dream of wearing chanel perfume, but - throw me in front of the chipmunks - I tried many, but I never was a chanel gal, I was always into Guerlain scents. Next day my husband surprised with this beauty (without me telling about my dream I saw).<br />
<br />
About the scent: I own the original chance, Fraiche, allure, allure sensuel, mademoiselle and noir (as I said I always wanted to like the house, never could) - eau tendre is high quality, but missing the patchuli undertone that makes most of the chanels smell like a stylish old lady. <br />
<br />
Fraiche and tendre are for young women. While I like Fraiche, it is too unisex, I can see easily on my husband. Tendre is feminim, almost like a fragile young girl, who has a surprisingly high IQ and big opinions. She stopes the room when she talks. <br />
<br />
I don't see it as mainstream. Black opium, libre, Mon guerlain, flower bomb are patchuli loaded vanillas, gucci guilty and bloom strait up florals. Cloud, and Baccarat Rouge and the molecular scent are leaning into clean unisex direction. <br />
<br />
I adore that Tendre stayed feminim, has a clean girl aesthetic and also has an extreme good staying power and sillage for what it is. <br />
Perfectly cut jeans, white shirt pair of pearl studs. <br />
No fake lashes, extension and tattoos. Just using what mama gave you. And having confidence to do so, and that makes it extremely appealing. Not trying too hard.<br />
<br />
I also got it, that it has a shampoo/shower aspect, but the amber makes the drydown extremely sexy and elegant. <br />
<br />
It has more uniqueness and mystery as Baccarat Rouge and gets far more compliments from men. <br />
User tip: buy 150 ml package, it is the best value, for your $$$.<br />
<br />
Fun fact, grapefruit smelling scents are making people guess your age younger. <br />
<br />
All in all my perfect signature scent. As my husband said when he gave it to me, he wants our daughter to grow up smelling this on mama. (She loves it too).<br />
<br />
One alarming comment: I could hardly wait to have the edp as it came out. What a disappointment. Lost the beauty of this gem, sillage and longevity is worse than the edt. Never again. I will use to layer at times.<br />
<br />
I love the hair mist though, it makes a great complement to the EDT and I gather even more compliments with it. <br />
<br />
If you want to smell divine, and stand out of the crowd buy this and never tell anyone what you wear! 🤣</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="8069"comment_id="1809270"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Chance-Eau-Tendre-8069.html?ccid=1809270#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1808893" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:1,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I used to wear this when I was dating my now husband and he does not like it. Does not hate, but does like.<br />
<br />
This is very similar to Mojave Ghost, I have a spritz of Chance Eau Tendre on one arm and Mojave Ghost on the other.<br />
Opening-Chance is more floral with some juiciness whereas Mojave is more juicy with a subtle floral backdrop<br />
Mid-Chance becomes more fresh and less floral and a soapy/shampooey effect, Mojave is more linear and continues to have a tangy/juicy fruitiness with some floral<br />
Dry down-Chance remains a clean, sparkling shampoo and Mojave turns sour on me <br />
<br />
I think Chance Eau Tendre is superior to Mojave Ghost for that reason. Mojave out shines Chance in the opening, but the dry down of Chance is much more pleasant, clean, and remains fresh whereas as Mojave turns sour to me. It could be the sandalwood in Mojave Ghost.<br />
<br />
Haven't owned this in over a decade but I may need to re-purchase the small bottle of this to have in my collection.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="8069"comment_id="1808733"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Chance-Eau-Tendre-8069.html?ccid=1808733#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1806480" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:1,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I mean, my biggest love is discontinued so this is the number one out of existing ones;) The fragrance is pretty versatile but I'd never wear it for work or during cloudy, ugly day when I feel depressed. Because it is the scent meant to cherish a good day, this is just too dreamy for unhappy circumstances.<br />
<br />
I'd  never guess it has jasmine, wood and musk - these are prominent notes but they are not there. It's not they vanish over time - they literally do not exist for me here. This is a subtle dance of quince&amp;grapefruit duo, accompanied with violet flowers. I am so much into it, already on the second bottle. <br />
<br />
Surprisingly, the fragrance works well for the night time too - it reveals its sexy side. Sexy in an efortless, non-offensive way: it wasn't meant to be sexy but somehow it plays tricks with my mind to the point no other 'loud' or 'dramatic' perfumes could do.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1330536">Sweetcove</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-04-04">04/04/23 21:42</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>A lot of people are dismissing this fragrance saying it’s too mainstream, too simple or not unique.<br />
But that’s exactly why I love chance eau tendre. It is simple, easy to wear, like a second skin. It is so loveable, so soft and so comforting. I don’t always want complexity and uniqueness. In fact, for my everyday life, I crave simplicity, ease, comfort and softness.<br />
When first applied, it smells clean and effervescent. Like a bubble bath. Then it warms up on the skin, becomes musky, powdery and creamy. It reminds me of the smell of a soft and clean baby skin (I know, weird 😅). <br />
<br />
Also, a lot of reviewers complain about longevity. This beauty is long lasting but : 1/it is loaded with musk, and it can create nose fatigue or you can also be anosmic to it. 2/it’s created this way, to be kind of fleeting, like its name : luck (chance) comes and goes. This perfume is the same, just when you think it has disappeared, you catch a whiff of it. 3/it’s long lasting, yes, but not projecting a lot. It’s a skin scent, quite intimate. It whispers and leaves a subtle trail behind you.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="8069"comment_id="1800794"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Chance-Eau-Tendre-8069.html?ccid=1800794#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1796963" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It may be the peary quince (because there are no real gourmand notes) but this scent opens and closes slightly sweet even in its soapiness. Floral and woodsy in the complimenting notes, it maintains a booming sillage despite being EDT. I will say that for me it has changed somewhat through the years, most notably becoming more dilute, but I feel like this happens when a scent expands to have a parfum or absolu.  This version of Chance feels like the rebel child of the Chanel Fragrance Family and I can only tolerate her sometimes, but every time I reach for her I get compliments. My favorite part is the drydown. Once the woodsy citrus and fruity quince fade a bit, the floral bouquet of hyacinth gives a long-lasting, bright finish that radiates for a while until it’s back to a sweet soapy ending. No wonder it’s the most popular Chance!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="8069"comment_id="1725433"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Chance-Eau-Tendre-8069.html?ccid=1725433#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1724851" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:1,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; ...with smile and class.<br />
<br />
EDIT: Guys love it!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="8069"comment_id="188048"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Chance-Eau-Tendre-8069.html?ccid=188048#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent213412" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc213412" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="tbear"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/132516"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.132516.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="tbear" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Chanel/Chance-Eau-Tendre-8069.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.8069.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Chance Eau Tendre"title="Chance Eau Tendre"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma213412ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck9x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd213412" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.71); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/132516">tbear</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2012-01-07">01/07/12 12:11</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I will preface this by confessing that I have not worn a fragrance since the 80's.  I am now in my 50's, happy and content except for the extra pounds I've gained this year.  I am working on taking off those pounds, but in the meantime, I felt like I needed a bit of a psychological lift.  Over the past few weeks I have made it my mission to find a fragrance that would do that for me.  After a lot of sampling, and not finding any fragrance my husband and I BOTH liked, I was almost convinced I would have to abandon my search.  But I am stubborn, and after finally seeking guidance from a knowledgeable SA, I took home four samples, one of which was Chance Eau Tendre.  I tried it and really liked it, and much to my surprise, my husband said he liked it too and would actually be able to enjoy this one!  (There were others he said he could tolerate, but that wasn't enough for me.)  So, I immediately ran right out and bought the 100ml size and I am so happy I did. <br />
<br />
I love the subtlety of the fruit and floral notes in Eau Tendre.  I did not want a fragrance that would surround me like a cloud, nor did I want to smell like overripe fruit, heady flowers, or candy.  Eau Tendre is light and feminine--just what I was looking for.  I also like that it stays pretty much the same, at least on me, and doesn't morph into something odd or funky after a few hours.  I am comfortable wearing this with jeans or wearing it out to dinner.  <br />
<br />
I didn't think I'd care about the bottle, but this one is gorgeous.  It's classic and elegant, and with its pale pink liquid, it looks beautiful sitting on my white vanity--a lovely bonus.<br />
<br />
For those who say that it doesn't last, I find that my nose definitely gets used to it after a few hours, but even when I can no longer detect it, my husband says he still can. He has told me several times how good I smell! <br />
<br />
Those who are devoted to Chanel will still have their classics.  But they were always too strong/heavy/powerful for me, which is why I initially bypassed the Chanel counter.  I am delighted that Chanel created this one for those of us who prefer something a little softer and lighter.  I definitely don't see it as just another copy of all the other fruity-florals out there, most of which are way too obvious and sweet for me.  (I tried a lot of them over the past few weeks.)  I know others disagree with me, and that's okay.  Fragrance preferences are highly subjective, and it would be a boring world if we all liked the same things.  But I know what I like and what my husband likes, and this is it!  Yay!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="8069"comment_id="213412"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Chance-Eau-Tendre-8069.html?ccid=213412#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent130001" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; There is nothing sexy about this, just childish, feminine innocence, in a very upscale style. If I didn't know, would I guess this is a Chanel? Absolutely not, this scent surely doesn't have much "chanelish" character. But it's an absolutely charismatic perfume, a little breeze of perfection, and I adore it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="8069"comment_id="130001"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Chance-Eau-Tendre-8069.html?ccid=130001#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent621330" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; My friend does only a couple sprays, and yet she is in a sweet powdery cloud, but there is nothing fresh about it. That cloud nags me, as it is constant and never changing, just sweet dusty musk. I think that it is pretty unique though, I can't remember any other fragrance that is almost a dupe.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="8069"comment_id="957115"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Chance-Eau-Tendre-8069.html?ccid=957115#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent457009" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc457009" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Mortazuma"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/656311"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.656311.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Mortazuma" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Chanel/Coco-Noir-15963.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.15963.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Coco Noir"title="Coco Noir"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma457009ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd457009" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.81); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/656311">Mortazuma</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2014-02-14">02/14/14 06:16</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Well Chance, we meet again. I didn't like your sister, and thought you might be different, but no. <br />
<br />
My apologies to all the ladies who happen to adore this fragrance, this review is not intended for you but is merely my experience of this fragrance with MY body chemistry. Needless to say, it didn't go well.<br />
<br />
The fragrance lacks the sophistication that one would expect from such a prestigious background. Is Mr. Polge losing his sense of smell or something? I certainly hope not. I have a suspicion that they skimped on the quality alcohol and used some synthetics because this (and Chance) is so far the only Chanel fragrance that I have actually felt an onset of a headache with. Maybe that is why this was called *Chance? It has that air of uncertainty, lack of confidence yet seems to be forcing its presence into the public by being somewhat shrill in hopes everyone will like it? I'M FROM CHANEL...YOU GOTTA LOVE ME!!!!<br />
<br />
Curiously, I know a few young women exactly like that...and they also liked this perfume. Perhaps it is not coincidence after all? <br />
<br />
<br />
* I know it was named Chance for the french meaning of Luck, but I fail to see the luck in this one.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="8069"comment_id="457009"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Chance-Eau-Tendre-8069.html?ccid=457009#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1013318" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1013318" class="cell small-2" ><div ><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Joys of life"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1169858"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1169858.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Joys of life" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Chanel/Jersey-Eau-de-Parfum-41776.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.41776.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Jersey Eau de Parfum"title="Jersey Eau de Parfum"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1013318ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1013318" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"><div class="flex-child-shrink" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.75); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1169858">Joys of life</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2018-12-25">12/25/18 20:44</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Very light and powdery, sweet, fruity floral. A person below described it as smelling similar to herbal essences shampoo and I can see where they’re coming from. There’s something this has in common with scented plastic toys and Victoria’s Secret body sprays that is off putting to me. Smells nice, clean, and market friendly.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="8069"comment_id="1013318"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Chance-Eau-Tendre-8069.html?ccid=1013318#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="8069" sentiment="negative"></reviews-infinity>
